- 08 Sep 2007
- 21 Oct 2003

- Years: 2007 - 2003 = 4 years
- Months: Sep (9) - Oct (10) = -1 month (or 11 months difference, since Sep is after Oct in the previous year)
- Days: 8 - 21 = -13 days

Or, in total years: roughly 3.86 years 😊

09/01/2026, 00:36 - Mehul: @⁨Meta AI⁩ what is giloda (vegitable name in Gujarati) called in hindi
09/01/2026, 00:36 - Dimp: Giloda (ગીલોડા) is a Gujarati term, and it's also known as Giloy or Guduchi in Hindi 😊

The Hindi name for Giloda is *गिलोय* (Giloy) or *गुडूची* (Guduchi)

It's a type of herbaceous vine, scientifically known as Tinospora cordifolia, commonly used in Ayurvedic medicine and cooking 🧘‍♀️
